Emerging growth company <span style="font-family:Times New Roman"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="duration_2021-11-30_to_2021-11-30" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></span></p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act. <span style="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9744;</span></p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p></div></div> <p style='page-break-before:always'></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" /> <div style="text-align:center"> <div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto"> <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;5.07. Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">On November&#160;30, 2021, Microsoft Corporation (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) held its 2021 Annual Shareholders Meeting (the &#8220;Annual Meeting&#8221;). There were 7,507,897,348 shares of common stock entitled to be voted at the Annual Meeting, of which 6,409,615,083 were voted in person or by proxy. The results for each item submitted for a vote of shareholders are as follows. The shareholders:</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(1) Voted to elect each of the twelve (12)&#160;nominees for director.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(2) Approved, on an advisory basis, the compensation of the Company&#8217;s named executive officers.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(3) Approved the Microsoft Employee Stock Purchase Plan</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(4) Voted to ratify the appointment of Deloitte&#160;&amp; Touche LLP as the Company&#8217;s independent registered public accounting firm for fiscal year 2022.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(5) Rejected a shareholder proposal concerning a report on<span style="font-weight:bold">&#160;</span>median pay gaps across race and gender.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(6) Approved a shareholder proposal concerning a report on the effectiveness of workplace sexual harassment policies.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(7) Rejected a shareholder proposal to prohibit sales of facial recognition technology to all government entities.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(8) Rejected a shareholder proposal concerning a report on<span style="font-weight:bold">&#160;</span>the implementation of the Fair Chance Business Pledge.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(9) Rejected a shareholder proposal concerning a report on how lobbying activities align with Company policies.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company&#8217;s inspector of election certified the following vote tabulations:</p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold">Election of Directors</p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
